---
title: "Buyer Screening"
---

Scored buyers for a defined target company.

NOTE: This is a asynchronous API, which means it will return a request\_id in the response. You would be required to poll the status and then retrieve the results. Read more about async APIs [here](https://docs.wokelo.ai/how-async-apis-work).

## Request reference

Here is a sample request containing all the parameters:

<CodeGroup>

```json cURL expandable wrap
curl --location 'https://api.wokelo.ai/api/enterprise/buyer-screening/enrich/' \
--header 'Authorization: Bearer Token' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--data '{
  "company": "acme-security",
  "parameters": {
    "detailed_query": "Looking for strategic acquirers in enterprise software",
    "buyer_type": ["strategic"],
    "company_type": "public",
    "geography": ["United States"]
  }
}'
```

```json Python expandable wrap
import requests
import json

url = "https://api.wokelo.ai/api/enterprise/buyer-screening/enrich/"

payload = json.dumps({
  "company": "acme-security",
  "parameters": {
    "detailed_query": "Looking for strategic acquirers in enterprise software",
    "buyer_type": [
      "strategic"
    ],
    "company_type": "public",
    "geography": [
      "United States"
    ]
  }
})
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer Token',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
```

</CodeGroup>

The table below lists all the parameters available to filter the results.

| Parameter | Description |
| :-- | :-- |
| `company` | Permalink or URL of the target company (e.g. `"acme-solar"` or `https://www.acmesolar.in/`) |
| `parameters.detailed_query` | A descriptive query to refine the buyer search scope and strategic criteria |
| `parameters.buyer_type` | Type of buyer to target: `"strategic"` or `"financial"` |
| `parameters.company_type` | Type of company to include: `"private"`, `"public"`, or `"all"` |
| `parameters.geography` | Geographic scope as ISO country codes (e.g. `["USA", "GBR"]`) |

## Examples

**Board-level buyer universe:** Find strategic acquirers for Brex — public companies in spend management, corporate cards, and CFO workflow software with mid-market and enterprise distribution.

### Sample Request

<CodeGroup>

```json cURL expandable wrap
curl --location 'https://api.wokelo.ai/api/enterprise/buyer-screening/enrich/' \
--header 'Authorization: Bearer Token' \
--header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
--data '{
  "company": "brex",
  "parameters": {
    "detailed_query": "Looking for companies in spend management, corporate cards, and CFO workflow software with mid-market and enterprise distribution",
    "buyer_type": "strategic",
    "company_type": "public",
    "geography": ["USA"]
  }
}'
```

```json Python expandable wrap
import requests
import json

url = "https://api.wokelo.ai/api/enterprise/buyer-screening/enrich/"

payload = json.dumps({
  "company": "brex",
  "parameters": {
    "detailed_query": "Looking for companies in spend management, corporate cards, and CFO workflow software with mid-market and enterprise distribution",
    "buyer_type": "strategic",
    "company_type": "public",
    "geography": [
      "USA"
    ]
  }
})
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer Token',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
```

</CodeGroup>


## Best practices

- Always fill in parameters.detailed\_query — it is the most important signal for result quality and relevance.
- Use sample\_companies to anchor the search around known players and guide the algorithm toward the right sub-market.
- Combine multiple filters (funding\_stage \+ geography \+ employee\_count) for precise deal sourcing rather than broad searches.
